commit 07727b79471535c7843827db03e7a5c182a0523e
Author: Anders Melander <anders@melander.dk>
Date:   2024-05-06 16:08:35 +0200

    Two new multi-threaded rasterizers has been introduced based on the PPL:
    
    TParallelRegularRasterizer uses TParallel.For and TTaskRegularRasterizer uses TTask with manual partitioning.
    Both vastly outperforms the old TThread-based TMultithreadedRegularRasterizer which has now been renamed TThreadRegularRasterizer and deprecated (for XE7 and later). TMultithreadedRegularRasterizer is now an alias for TParallelRegularRasterizer when that is available (XE7 and later).

commit ec6e496f7e29b83c30282d3589079561850563b8
Author: Anders Melander <anders@melander.dk>
Date:   2023-04-23 22:20:56 +0200

    The paint-stage flags DsgnTime and RunTime has been deprecated. Instead we now have a "mask set" that indicates what the paint stage should be used for: psmRunTime, psmDesignTime and psmExport.
    psmRunTime replaces the DsgnTime flag, psmDesignTime replaces the DsgnTime flag and the new psmExport flag indicates if the paint stage should be drawn by the PaintTo method.
    Only the PST_DRAW_BITMAP and PST_DRAW_LAYERS paint-stages have the psmExport mask flag set by default.
    Fixes #247
    Fixes #248

commit a35ad730dcab92e3c514fb4d0d5f2adc4eaf5422

commit 53b18c30781f294f74b50a6a615eda2680313a98
Author: Anders Melander <anders@melander.dk>
Date:   2022-04-08 18:01:55 +0200

    Resample() optimization by Renate Schaaf:
    - Iterate pixels in YX order instead of XY order to avoid trashing the cache.
    Further Resample() optimizations:
    - Access channels in BGRA order corresponding to the physical order on Windows.
    - Removed old bit twiddling (on Win32 only) which turned out to be slightly slower on modern processors.
    - Replaced for loops with while loops where possible.
    Misc refactoring and reformat for readability.

    Finally a correct naming and handling of the gamma correction.
    Now, you can specify the gamma value as it is (e.g. 2.2). Based on this value the correct encoding and decoding tables are calculated. These are used internally correctly. This value should be specified just once according to the monitor. It's also possible to specify sRGB, which is nowadays the standard.

    * improved Grow() function for jsRound even further. It is now between 140% (small line widths) and 25% (large line widths) faster than the original version with joints rounder than the original implementation. commit 73dba71808beaf66267fe866086d114da668cbfa
Author: micha137 <bunk@iat.uni-leipzig.de>
Date:   2010-11-23 16:50:56 +0000

    Prevent a race (crash) during startup, add Multithreaded Regular Rasterizer to menu
    
    The Race
    --------
    
    The race was caused by the property loading starting the render thread while load was still in progress.  The render thread tried to render an image with the dimensions of the TSyntheticImage, with Width = 460 and Height = 412.  Unfortunately TSyntheticImage32.FBuffer had allocated only memory for a 192x192 image.  If the render thread was faster than the FBuffer reallocation, we got memory access violations.
    
    The solution involves deferring the call to SelectRasterizer() from TMainForm.FormCreate() to TMainForm.FormShow().  This prevents the render thread from being
    started during property loading by the MainForm.FormCreate event.
    
    
    Menu changes
    ------------
    
    The menu items have AutoCheck=True.  If an already selected rasterizer menu entry was selected again, it became deselected!  So in
    TMainForm.RasterizerMenuClick I set Checked := True.
    
    TMultithreadedRegularRasterizer was added as a menu option.  This rasterizer is undocumented!
    
    
    Removed unused variables
    ------------------------
    
    AutoUpdate, pathMedia were unused on all platforms.

commit 6bfb6be9ecc79dd4c19191dc631ec7967122e576
Author: micha137 <bunk@iat.uni-leipzig.de>
Date:   2010-11-23 16:41:36 +0000

    Remove unused variable

commit 8f96d4c4256326a24b262fd2cf25d7464eeff94f
Author: micha137 <bunk@iat.uni-leipzig.de>
Date:   2010-11-23 16:40:35 +0000

    Start the render thread with the actual current buffer size
    
    This prevents rendering to places for which no buffer was allocated yet.  Normally, self.{Width,Height} and Buffer.{Width,Height} are equal.  Except during property loading at application start.  Then it is possible for self.{Width,Height} to contain the loaded properties of the form and Buffer.{Width,Height} to still contain the default values (192, 192).  If the render thread is started with a bigger rect than this, it could lead to memory access violations on a sufficiently fast machine or with weird timing exactly when rendering outside (192, 192) is done before the actual Buffer for it is allocated in the main thread.

commit 192fbcbfbfba8b3eb63a2a8e9ad097a4539430e3
Author: angusj <AngusJohnson@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   2009-10-17 21:37:25 +0000

    PAS file parsing now also accepts //* comments as specially flagged for importing into HTM documentation.
    
    Notes: consecutive lines of //* comments will be treated as one multi-line comment. Multi-line comments will appear as a single (word wrapped) line in the HTML documentation. To force a newline to appear in the documentation, an HTML <br> token must be added into the comment.

commit 298a167304dc460fe500fd5675cd5a9c6d852f5f
Author: angusj <AngusJohnson@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   2009-10-17 11:42:37 +0000

    The PAS file parser now converts specially crafted comment blocks - (** ... *) - into help document descriptions.
    
    In order for these comment blocks to be recognised, they must immediately precede class definitions, class methods and properties, function and procedure definitions and type definitions.

commit aa4b2a2757887b40e75a1116e89c51baf0a485d5
Author: mandersson <meanderix@gmail.com>
Date:   2005-06-22 19:34:26 +0000

    Extended the resampling framework with a set of new nested samplers:
    - TKernelSampler: base class for samplers that use a kernel or a structuring element to compute each sample;
    - TConvolver: a sampler that performs convolution;
    - TDilater: performs dilation;
    - TEroder: performs erosion;
    - TExpander, TContracter: similar to TDilater and TEroder, but weights are multiplied instead of added/subtracted;
    - TSafeSampler: anology to the safe pixel getters but implemented as a sampler.

commit c9a591ef3d7986cffe0eb498c45926069970a633
Author: pixedcom <info@pixed.com>
Date:   2005-05-28 09:09:14 +0000

    PROPOSAL CHECKIN! (Please read full comment)
    TPersepctiveTransf. has been corrected, and  true fixed versions has been added (its flying now!).
    Auxillary matrix conversion (float vs fixed) has been added.
    General cleanups.
    TConformalTransformation has been merged with TTransformation, and different precisioncallbacks (int, fixed, float) has been set up to call the next precision level (if not int then fixed, if not fixed then float), this takes place in TTransformation. Basically new decendants only need to implement float for it all to work. Abstract float versions has been exchanged with dummys that passes input to output - conceptually this is most coherent since TTransformation does no transformation.
    256 callback version has been removed! No part of the lib seems to use these anymore. If 256 is needed, a routine should call the fixed version and SAR_8 the results - this is not particulary slower.
    TIntegerMatrix has been changed to TFixedMatrix, and all "small" fixed versions has been changed to true fixed mode.
    I'm not fully aware of eventual compatibility issues.. Andre, please don't kill me.
    Last thing: affine seems to handle src rect wrongly... changing srcrect causes result displacement - this is not true for other transformations.. can any of you confirm this as a bug?
